<P STYLE="text-align: center; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: right"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: center; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><IMG SRC="ex99-1_001.jpg" ALT=""></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: center; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: justify; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><B>FG Nexus Further Enhances Governance and Appoints Scott D. Wollney as
Lead Independent Director</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify"><B>Charlotte, NC &ndash; December 8, 2025 &ndash;
</B>FG Nexus Inc. (Nasdaq: FGNX, FGNXP<B>) </B>(the &ldquo;Company&rdquo;), today announced the appointment of Scott D. Wollney as Lead
Independent Director of the Company&rsquo;s Board of Directors. Mr. Wollney has served as a director of the Company for the past 10 years,
and currently chairs the Audit Committee and is a member of the Compensation &amp; Management Resources Committee.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">Mr. Wollney brings over 30 years of experience in
the financial services industry. He currently serves as President, Chief Executive Officer, and Director of Atlas Financial Holdings,
Inc., a specialty commercial insurance holding company. Mr. Wollney holds an MBA from Northwestern University&rsquo;s Kellogg School of
Management with a concentration in finance and management strategy, and a Bachelor of Arts degree from the University of Illinois.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">&ldquo;Scott&rsquo;s extensive experience in financial
services, combined with his deep understanding of our business, makes him ideally suited to serve as our Lead Independent Director,&rdquo;
said Kyle Cerminara, Chairman &amp; CEO of FG Nexus. &ldquo;His leadership will be invaluable as we continue to execute our ETH treasury
strategy.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify"><B>FG Nexus </B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">FG Nexus (Nasdaq: FGNX, FGNXP) (the &ldquo;Company&rdquo;)
is focused on building a digital asset treasury and a leading platform for the tokenization of real-world assets. To enhance the yield
on its treasury, the Company will stake its ETH and implement additional yield strategies while positioning itself as a strategic gateway
into digital-asset-powered finance, including tokenized RWAs and stablecoin-based yield solutions.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">The FGNX<SUP>&reg; </SUP>logo is a registered trademark.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>
